+static void tps65994_check_version(struct tps65994 *tps)
+{
+	struct i2c_client *client = tps->i2c_client;
+	char custuse[9] = { };
+	char ver_str[9] = { };
+	char *ver_ptr;
+	int ret;
+	int kernel_version = 0, eeprom_version = 0;
+	bool update_needed = false;
+
+	ret = tps65994_i2c_read(client, TPS_REG_CUSTUSE, custuse, NULL);
+	if (ret) {
+		dev_err(&client->dev, "failed to read custuse
");
+		return;
+	}
+
+	if (!strncmp(PATCH_VER_HEADER, custuse, PATCH_VER_HEADER_LEN)) {
+		ver_ptr = strnstr(tps6598x_lowregion_array_gandalf,
+				  PATCH_VER_HEADER, gSizeLowregionArrayGandalf);
+		if (ver_ptr != NULL) {
+			memcpy(ver_str, ver_ptr, 8);
+			if (ver_str[4] > custuse[4]) {
+				update_needed = true;
+			} else {
+				ret = kstrtol(ver_str + 6, 10, &kernel_version);
+				if (ret) {
+					dev_err(&client->dev, "kstrtol get kernel_version failed
");
+					return;
+				}
+				ret = kstrtol(custuse + 6, 10, &eeprom_version);
+				if (ret) {
+					dev_err(&client->dev, "kstrtol get eeprom_version failed
");
+					return;
+				}
+				if (kernel_version > eeprom_version)
+					update_needed = true;
+			}
+		} else
+			update_needed = true;
+	} else
+		update_needed = true;
+
+	if (update_needed) {
+		dev_info(&client->dev, "newer version detected:
");
+		dev_info(&client->dev, "current version: %s
", custuse);
+		dev_info(&client->dev, "new version: %s
", ver_str);
+		ret = tps65994_write_eeprom(tps, 0, SOURCE_INTERNAL);
+		if (ret)
+			dev_warn(tps->dev, "write image to EEPROM failed
");
+	} else {
+		dev_info(&client->dev, "current version: %s
", custuse);
+	}
+}
+

 	char mode[5] = { };
